# Dynamic MetaSprite ROM Address Debug
# MS_FS_DATA_BANK = 0xC1 (bank start: 0x0000)
# DYNAMIC_SPRITE_TILES_DATA_BANK = 0xC2 (base bank)

ROM Data (first 256 bytes):
  $0000: 2E 24 24 5C 08 36 00 98 18 26 27 26 56 08 74 19
  $0010: EB 49 2E 24 24 5B 08 8B 4B F7 63 2D 2A 28 56 08
  $0020: 3F 64 6B 94 2E 24 24 5C 08 FB 95 F3 A1 00 00 00
  $0030: 00 04 69 A2 BD A2 AB 00 0E 01 8A 01 FC 01 5F 02
  $0040: E0 02 4D 03 C9 03 40 04 AD 04 33 05 BE 05 3A 06
  $0050: BB 06 28 07 A9 07 25 08 BF 08 31 09 CB 09 38 0A
  $0060: A0 0A 12 0B 7F 0B E2 0B 45 0C A8 0C 0B 0D 87 0D
  $0070: F9 0D 5C 0E DD 0E 4A 0F C6 0F 3D 10 AA 10 30 11
  $0080: BB 11 37 12 B8 12 25 13 A6 13 22 14 BC 14 2E 15
  $0090: C8 15 35 16 9D 16 0F 17 7C 17 DF 17 42 18 00 04
  $00A0: 00 02 80 03 00 00 00 00 00 04 02 FF FF FF FF 2E
  $00B0: 24 24 5C 00 00 00 30 20 00 20 01 40 20 02 20 01
  $00C0: 30 30 04 20 01 40 30 06 20 01 50 30 08 20 01 30
  $00D0: 40 0A 20 01 40 40 0C 20 01 50 40 0E 20 01 30 50
  $00E0: 20 20 01 40 50 22 20 01 30 60 24 20 01 40 60 26
  $00F0: 20 01 30 70 28 20 01 40 70 2A 20 01 FF 00 00 00

=== bred.Bred ===
Frameset header at: $C10000
  +4,5 = frameTable pointer
  +6,7 = animationTable pointer
